Row[2] = 86 year old female with history of right hip osteoarthritis that is s/p right hip arthroplasty on 6/30/17 with Dr. Fowler.  CIC consulted for postop medical management.  Post op patient had N/V and was also noted to have difficulty swallowing.  ST eval showed no frank aspiration but did show gurgling with water.  GI was consulted and pt had EGD 7/1 which showed esophageal stricture, food was moved passed stricture, plans for outpt f/u EGD for dilation, no meat products at discharge.  Pt also with postop blood loss anemia and is s/p 1U of PRBCs, hgb 7.4 as of 7/3/17.  Patient became hypoxic with patchy infiltrates after her N/V issues priors to EGD.  She was started on clindamycin empirically.  She developed CP, and EKG was checked 7/3 with some abormalities.  Susbsequent troponins were elevated adynamically.  Cardiology was consulted, TTE returned with EF of 45%, mod-severe MR with previously only mild MR.  Some segmental wall motion abnromalities were noted of the LV.  Pt was diuresed with IV lasix with good improvement of respiratory status and mitral murmur.  Had duplex negative for DVT, study performed on 7/3.  Finished course of clindamycin for aspiration pneumonia.  Hemoglobin drifting down, therefore, transfused 2 units PRBC on 7/9/17 per Cardiology.
